get a (pointer) value (explicit) 

Performs explicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value if required.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the requested type is a pointer to the internally stored JSON value that pointer is returned. No copies are made.
\item If the requested type is the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}}, or a different \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} convertible from the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}}.
\item Otherwise the value is converted by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenlohmann_1_1detail_aef5c8ea108f4d2b03fb4a635617510de}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Paramètres du template}
{\em Value\+Type\+CV} & the provided value type \\
\hline
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
copy of the JSON value, converted to 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Paramètres du template}
{\em Value\+Type} & if necessary\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_ad6ebc5da7ced975bb184133750e7d49f}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenlohmann_1_1detail_aef5c8ea108f4d2b03fb4a635617510de}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method throws if conversion is required\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

auto \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) -\/$>$ decltype(std\+::declval$<$basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t\&$>$().template \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr}}$<$Pointer\+Type$>$())     \hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



get a pointer value (explicit) 

Explicit pointer access to the internally stored JSON value. No copies are made.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Avertissement}
The pointer becomes invalid if the underlying JSON object changes.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Paramètres du template}
{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a858c1cf8407bc06494e3a1114a3b73e7}{array\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_aef3ff5a73597850597d1d40db9edd376}{object\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a33593865ffb1860323dcbd52425b90c8}{string\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a44fd1a12c9c54623c942b430e7a72937}{boolean\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a11e390944da90db83089eb2426a749d3}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_ae09af9c23351b7245d9be4d1b2035fef}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a5b8abaebd922d82d69756327c0c347e6}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
pointer to the internally stored JSON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the JSON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a JSON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a85222410e03d8f5c8ff9c78cf9f6b1b6}{get\+\_\+ptr()}} for explicit pointer-\/member access
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1conjunction}{detail\+::conjunction}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1json__ref}{detail\+::json\+\_\+ref}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1is__basic__json}{detail\+::is\+\_\+basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::initializer\+\_\+list$<$ typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structnlohmann_1_1detail_1_1is__detected__lazy}{detail\+::is\+\_\+detected\+\_\+lazy}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacenlohmann_1_1detail_ab4d22cdb6521ee3508db496dea66711e}{detail\+::get\+\_\+template\+\_\+function}}, const basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t \&, Value\+Type $>$ $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a11641b35219676b225d9bd15c7677659}{\+::value}}, int $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a5b7c4b35a0ad9f97474912a08965d7ad}{\+::type}}  = 0$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{json_8hpp_aefed8cf27cadeea45f12c6f3db3ce774}{JSON\+\_\+\+EXPLICIT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json}{nlohmann\+::basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type $>$\+::operator Value\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



get a value (implicit) 

Implicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value. The call is realized by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_af1650e004db368459b3c0db041b32adc}{get() const}}.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Paramètres du template}
{\em Value\+Type} & non-\/pointer type compatible to the JSON value, for instance {\ttfamily int} for JSON integer numbers, {\ttfamily bool} for JSON booleans, or {\ttfamily std\+::vector} types for JSON arrays. The character type of \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a33593865ffb1860323dcbd52425b90c8}{string\+\_\+t}} as well as an initializer list of this type is excluded to avoid ambiguities as these types implicitly convert to {\ttfamily std\+::string}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
copy of the JSON value, converted to type {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em type\+\_\+error.\+302} & in case passed type {\itshape Value\+Type} is incompatible to the JSON value type (e.\+g., the JSON value is of type boolean, but a string is requested); see example below\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@complexity Linear in the size of the JSON value.

@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from JSON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A JSON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}short\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}\textbackslash{}, (3) A JSON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}.,operator\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Obsolète}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000005}{Obsolète}}]This stream operator is deprecated since 3.\+0.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. Please use \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_aea0de29387d532e0bc5f2475cb83995d}{operator$>$$>$(std\+::istream\&, basic\+\_\+json\&)}} instead; that is, replace calls like {\ttfamily j \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} i;} with {\ttfamily i \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} j;}. \end{DoxyRefDesc}

\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000003}{Obsolète}}]This function is deprecated since 3.\+0.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. Please use \mbox{\hyperlink{classnlohmann_1_1basic__json_a5bbe57177fdb5833885dc1567ec13394}{operator$<$$<$(std\+::ostream\&, const basic\+\_\+json\&)}} instead; that is, replace calls like {\ttfamily j \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} o;} with {\ttfamily o \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} j;}. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
